### ALLOW FOREIGN SS UNITS
country_event = {

	id = 91000
		
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	title = "EVTNAME91000"
	desc = "EVTDESC91000"
	picture = "EVT94038"

	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA91000" # ok
		set_country_flag = foreign_SS_units_decision
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "foreign_SS_units"
			duration = 1100
		}
		manpower = 50
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB91000"  # no
		set_country_flag = foreign_SS_units_decision
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

### ALLOW Division upgrades/Luftwaffe reorg
country_event = {

	id = 866635
		
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		year = 1936
		not = { has_country_flag = upgrades_yes }
		not = { has_country_flag = upgrades_no }
	}
	
	title = "Wehrmacht Upgrade Events"
	desc = "EVTDESC866635"
	picture = "evtpicture14840"

	
	option = {
		name = "Allow the events" # ok
		set_country_flag = upgrades_yes
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "unique_wehrmacht_units"
			duration = 3000
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "No Thanks"  # no
		set_country_flag = upgrades_yes
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "no_wehrmacht_units"
			duration = 3000
		}
		set_country_flag = upgrades_no
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = 95071
	
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		date = 1936.1.24
		war = no
		not = { has_country_flag = flag_pre_olym_games }
		not = { has_country_flag = flag_pre_olym_games_no }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	title = "Preparation for Winter Olympic Games 1936"
	desc = "EVTDESC95071"
	picture = "GER_winolyg"

		name = "Ready?"
		supplies = -15000

	}

country_event = {

	id = 95002
	
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		date = 1936.2.6
		not = { year = 1937 }
		war = no

# Closing Cerenomy #
country_event = {
	id = 95004
	
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		date = 1936.2.16
		war = no
		has_country_flag = winter_olympics_1936
		not = { has_country_flag = flag_closing_ceremony }
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	title = "Closing ceremony Olympic Winter Games 1936"
	desc = "EVTDESC95004"
	picture = "GER_woc1936"
	
	option = {
		name = "Germany"
		threat = {
			who = all
			value = -5
		}
		manpower = 6
		money = 200
		set_country_flag = flag_closing_ceremony
		mountain_warfare_equipment = 10
        artic_warfare_equipment = 10

        ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

	id = 9032
	
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		date = 1937.5.6
		not = { has_country_flag = hindenburg_crash }
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME9032"
	desc = "EVTDESC9032"
	picture = "airship"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA9032"
		GER = { dissent = 5 }
		set_country_flag = hindenburg_crash
		GER = {
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = "hindenburg_crash"
				duration = 60
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		USA = { country_event = 9035 }
	}
}

	id = 91182

		tag = GER
		head_of_government = 2 #Rudolf Hess
		date = 1941.5.10
		1567 = { controlled_by = ENG }
		not = { has_country_flag = last_flight_hess }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		days = 1
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME91182"
	desc = "EVTDESC91182"

	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA91182" #Replace him with Bormann
		set_country_flag = last_flight_hess
		remove_minister = 2 #Rudolf Hess
		head_of_government = 42 #Bormann
		dissent = 4
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
}

#### Upgrade from 1. Geb.-Brigade to 1. Geb.-Division
country_event = {
	
	id = 400038

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	title = "Form the 1. Geb.-Division"
	desc = "EVTDESC400038"
	picture = "1-Gebdiv"

	option = {
		name = "Creation of 1. Gebirgsjäger-Division "
		remove_brigade = "Geb.-Rgt. 99/100"
		remove_brigade = "Geb.-Art.-Rgt. 69"
		remove_brigade = "Gefechtstross-Bat. 54"
		set_country_flag = gebdiv_one
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
        OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = GER has_country_flag = BlackICE
					total_ic = 150
					not = { total_ic = 200 }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "5IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_150_III"
					duration = 90
				}	
				load_oob = GER/GER_1_GebirgsDiv_build.txt
			}
		}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	title = "ZG 142 'Horst Wessel'"
	desc = "EVTDESC1054"
	picture = "ZG142"
	
	option = {
		name = "Forming the ZG 142 'Horst Wessel' "
		
		remove_brigade = "III/JG 134"
		remove_brigade = "I/JG 134"
		remove_brigade = "II/JG 134"
		remove_brigade = "IV/JG 134"
		
		set_country_flag = ZG142
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
        OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = GER has_country_flag = BlackICE
					total_ic = 150
					not = { total_ic = 200 }
				}

		tag = GER
		not = { has_country_flag = deutschland_class_ca }
		not = { has_country_flag = deutschland_class_ca_no }

		heavycruiser_armament = 4
		heavycruiser_engine = 4
		heavycruiser_armour = 4
	}
	
	title = "Reclassifying the Deutschland Class Panzerschiffe"
	desc = "EVTDESC400043"
	picture = "GER_Admiral_Scheer_in_Gibraltar"

		name = "Reclassifying Deutschland Class Panzerschiffe"
		set_country_flag = deutschland_class_ca
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = {
		name = "Continue Building Deutschland Class Panzerschiffe"
		set_country_flag = deutschland_class_ca_no
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

## NUREMBERG RALLY - 1936
country_event = {

	id = 91171
		
	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		date = 1936.9.14
		war = no
		ideology = national_socialist
		not = { has_country_flag = nuremberg_rally_1936 }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		days = 1
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME91171"
	desc = "EVTDESC91171"
	picture = "nuremberg_rally_1936"

	option = {
		name = "Reichsparteitag der Ehre"
		set_country_flag = nuremberg_rally_1936
		supplies = -2500
		organisation = 5
		popularity = 5
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "industry_works"
			duration = 30
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "propaganda"
			duration = 360
		}
		random_owned = {
			limit = {
				not = { industry = 8 }
			}
			industry = 2
		}
		random_owned = { limit = { not = { industry = 8 } } industry = 2 }
		relation = { who = SOV value = -10 }
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}
	option = {

	id = 90150
	
	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		not = { faction = axis }
		not = { faction = allies }
		not = { faction = comintern }
		not = { war_with = GER }
		not = { war_with = JAP }
		has_global_flag = tripartite_pact
		not = { has_global_flag = tripartite_pact_NO }
		not = { has_country_flag = tripartite_pact_joinITA }
		not = { has_country_flag = tripartite_pact_leaveITA }
	}
	
	title = "EVTNAME90149"
	desc = "EVTDESC90149"
	picture = "tripartite_pact"
	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA90150"
		join_faction = axis
		ITA = {	
			war = {	
				target = ENG
				attacker_goal = { casus_belli = conquer }
			}
		}
		#war = FRA # This is redundant as England and France are in Allies together
		set_country_flag = tripartite_pact_joinITA
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
	}	
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA90130"
		ITA = { relation = { who = GER value = -30 } }
		ITA = { threat = { who = GER value = 20 } }
		GER = { relation = { who = ITA value = -30 } }
		GER = { threat = { who = ITA value = 20 } }
		set_country_flag = tripartite_pact_leaveITA
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
	}
}

### Convert Liner
country_event = {

	id = 88080
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	title = "EVTNAME88080"
	desc = "EVTDESC88080"

		set_country_flag = converted_liner

				limit = { tag = GER has_country_flag = BlackICE
					total_ic = 150

## Great patriotic war
country_event = {

	id = 49294

	trigger = {
		tag = GER
		ai = no
		not =  {has_global_flag = NO_MODIFIERS }
		not = { has_global_flag = EastNoob }
		or = {
			and = {
				month = 11
				year = 1941
					}
			and = {
					year = 1942
					not = { month = 2 }
					not = { month = 3 }
					not = { month = 4 }
					not = { month = 5 }
					not = { month = 6 }
					not = { month = 7 }
					not = { month = 8 }
					not = { month = 9 }
					not = { month = 10}
					}
				}
		
		not = { has_country_modifier = german_destiny }
		or = {
			SOV = { has_country_modifier = great_patriotic_war }
			SOV = { has_country_modifier = patriotic_war }
		}
		has_country_flag = destiny
		controls = 1694
		controls = 2223
		controls = 1178
		SOV = {
			controls = 1409 # Moscow
			controls = 782  # Leningrad
			controls = 2857 # Stalingrad
		}
		not = { has_country_flag = barbarossa_fail }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen =  {
		days = 1
	}

	title = "Winterschlacht Im Osten"
	desc = "EVTDESC49294"
	picture = "barbarossa_fails"

	option = {
		name = "God Help Us !"
		set_country_flag = barbarossa_fail
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "barb_fail"
			duration = 30
		}
	}
}

#### After the first excercises some flows came to light and there for the Brigade was transformed into the 1. Leichte Division on the 1 April 1938. ####

#### In October 1 Panzer Division was reorganized as part of the Wehrmacht's increase in the number of mechanized divisions. The 2nd Panzer Regiment and selected cadres were removed for the formation of the 16th Panzer Division. In compensation, the 113th Panzergrenadier Regiment was added to balance the divisional organization. ####

is_triggered_only = yes
	
	title = "3. Panzer-Divison"
	desc = "EVTDESC400019"
	picture = "3-Panzer"

	option = {
		name = "Form the 3. Panzer-Division "
		set_country_flag = 3_PzDiv
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		
        OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = GER has_country_flag = BlackICE
					total_ic = 150
					not = { total_ic = 200 }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "20IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_150_I"
					duration = 180
				}	
				load_oob = GER/GER_3_Pz_Div_build.txt
			}
		}
        OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = GER has_country_flag = BlackICE
					total_ic = 200
					not = { total_ic = 250 }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "20IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_200_I"
					duration = 180
				}	
				load_oob = GER/GER_3_Pz_Div_build.txt
			}
		}
        OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = GER has_country_flag = BlackICE
					total_ic = 250
					not = { total_ic = 300 }
				}

#### 3. Panzer In January 1941, in order to support the newly forming Afrika Korps, the division detached the 5th Panzer Regiment, the 3rd Motorized Reconnaissance Battalion, 39th Panzerjäger Battalion, and 1/75th Artillery Regiment. ####
country_event = {

	id = 49377
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	title = "3. Panzer-Divison 'Berliner Bären'"
	desc = "EVTDESC49377"
	picture = "3-Panzer"

	option = {
		name = "Refit the 3. Panzer-Division "
		set_country_flag = 3_mPzDiv
		
		remove_brigade = "Stab 3. Panzer-Division"

#### 4. Panzer Division was formed as 7th Panzer Brigade in Würzburg on 10 November 1935, as the first unit of the second series of German fast units. On 10 October 1938, it was upgraded to full divisional status. ####

#### 4. Panzer Division was refitted at her standort Wurzburg and the Pz.-Rgt 36 was transferred to the newly formed 14. Panzer Division auf den Truppenubunsplatz Milowitz, Konigsbruck. ####

#### 29. Motorised The first four motorized infantry divisions (2., 13., 20. and 29.) were directly upgraded from infantry divisions during 1937 to 1939, so they kept most of the features of their parent ones. Each motorized infantry division had three motorized infantry regiments plus one motorized artillery regiment as its major combat components, the division also had other supportive units. ####

#### 13. Motorised The first four motorized infantry divisions (2., 13., 20. and 29.) were directly upgraded from infantry divisions during 1937 to 1939, so they kept most of the features of their parent ones. Each motorized infantry division had three motorized infantry regiments plus one motorized artillery regiment as its major combat components, the division also had other supportive units ####
country_event = {

#### 20. Motorised The first four motorized infantry divisions (2., 13., 20. and 29.) were directly upgraded from infantry divisions during 1937 to 1939, so they kept most of the features of their parent ones. Each motorized infantry division had three motorized infantry regiments plus one motorized artillery regiment as its major combat components, the division also had other supportive units ####

		date = 1936.06.03
		war = no
		not = { has_country_flag = flag_ural }
	}

		days = 1
	}

	desc = "EVTDESC866633"
	picture = "wever"

		name = "Continue the Ural Bomber Program"
		set_country_flag = flag_strats
		set_country_flag = flag_ural
		kill_leader = 483 #wever
		
	}
	option = {
		name = "Focus on Tactical and Dive Bombers"
		set_country_flag = flag_tacs
		set_country_flag = flag_ural
		two_engine_bombbay = 150
		twin_engine_bomber_crew_layout = 150
		twin_engine_airframe = 150
		kill_leader = 483 #wever
		load_oob = Prototypes.txt
	}
}

country_event = {
	
	id = 38746

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
		
	title = "Panzershcreck"
	desc = "EVTDESC38746"   # The arrival of the T 34 increased numbers created increased strain on the Wehrmacht. One solution was increased 88mm guns on the frontlines.
	picture = "mass_production_t_34"

	option = {
		name = "Mein Gott Ja !!!" 		# rush 88s to the front lines !
        OMG = {
			any_country = {
				limit = { tag = GER has_country_flag = BlackICE
					total_ic = 150
					not = { total_ic = 200 }
				}
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = "10IC_Unit_spawn_penalty_150_V"
					duration = 90
				}	
				load_oob = Motorised_88mm.txt
			}
		}

## PANZER 5TH ARMY DEFENSE OF TUNIS - GERMAN Events by DAN
country_event = {

	id = 95555
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	title = "EVTNAME95555"
	desc = "EVTDESC95555"
	picture = "DAK"
	
	# Germany sends reinforcements
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTA95555"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "Panzer_5th_Army_Tunis_Defense_German"
			duration = 220
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		manpower = -200
		supplies = -15000
		fuel = -1000
		ITA = { country_event = 95556 }
		GER = {
			5134 = { # Tunis
				supplies = 15000
				fuel = 1000
			}
			load_oob = GER/GER_Panzer_5th_Army.txt
 		}
		set_country_flag = Panzer_5th_Army_Tunis_Defense_German
	}

	# Germany send Expeditionary Forces
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTB95555"
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = "Panzer_5th_Army_Tunis_Defense_Italian"
			duration = 220
		}
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		manpower = -200
		ITA = { country_event = 95557
			supplies = -5000
			fuel = -1000
			5134 = { # Tunis
				supplies = 5000
				fuel = 1000
			}
		
			load_oob = GER/GER_Panzer_5th_Army_EXP.txt # AS EXPEDITIONARY FORCE
 		}
		set_country_flag = Panzer_5th_Army_Tunis_Defense_Italian
	}

	# Germany sends nothing
	option = {
		name = "EVTOPTC95555"
		
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		set_country_flag = Panzer_5th_Army_Tunis_Defense_Declined
	}

}
